bba	bɑ sun tɑbu wɔri Yɑhɑsiɔ.

bba	kɑnɑru nɔ. U nɛɛ, yɑ turɑ mɛ. N

bba	win wirun tɑri yi mɛnnɑ kɑ wɛ̃ɛ
bba	siiri u wesɑ. Mɑ u kɑ yi dɑ̃ru
bba	kpɑresi temɔ. Yerɑ u nùn yɑmiɑ u
bba	nɛɛ, Sɑnsom, Filisitibɑ wee, bɑ
bba	N deemɑ Mikɑ u rɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ yeru mɔ
bba	win yɛnuɔ. Mɑ u derɑ bɑ nùn
bba	bwɑ̃ɑroku ɡɑnu kuɑ. Mɑ u win
bba	tiin bii turo ɡɔsɑ u kuɑ nin
bba	Mɑ Dɑnu be, bɑ ɡurenɑ bɑ doonɑ,
bba	bɑ ben bibu ɡbiisie kɑ yɑɑ sɑbenu

bba	kɛtɛkunu dĩɑnu wɛ̃. Ben tii bɑ
bba	ben nɑɑsu kpɑkiɑ, mɑ u bu dĩɑnu
bba	wɛ̃ bɑ dimɔ bɑ nɔrumɔ
bba	Mɑ Isireli be, bɑ dɑ Betɛliɔ bu
bba	kɑ Gusunɔ bikiɑ u bu sɔ̃ɔsi bwese
bba	kɛrɑ ye yɑ koo ɡbi yu
bba	Bɛnyɑmɛɛbɑ wɔri. Mɑ Yinni
bba	Gusunɔ u Yudɑbɑ ɡɔsɑ.
bba	Isirelibɑ bɑ ɡɔsirɑmɑ bɑ nɑ
bba	Bɛnyɑmɛɛ be bɑ tien wusu sɔɔ.

bba	sɑbenɔ. Hunde koni ye yɑ wɑ̃ɑ mi
bba	kpuro ɡesi, bɑ ɡowɑ. Mɑ bɑ ben
bba	wuu si kpuro dɔ̃ɔ mɛni.
bba	6-7 Yenibɑn biru, Nɑomi u nuɑ
bba	Gusunɔ u win tɔmbu durom kuɑ u bu
bba	dĩɑnu wɛ̃. Yerɑ u seewɑ sɔ̃ɔ
bba	teeru kɑ win biɡii kurɔbu Mɔɑbun

bba	kpɑ̃ɑru bo. Domi u nùn kĩ bɑɑ
bba	mɛ Yinni Gusunɔ u nùn kuɑ wĩro.
bba	U sɑ̃ɑwɑ nɡe kpee bɑɑ mi nɑ rɑ
bba	Adɑmɑ u koo de tɔn kɔ̃sobu

bba	ɡeruɑ mɑ wunɛn yɛnu kɑ wunɛn
bba	bɑɑbɑn yɛnuɡibu bɑ koo ko win

bba	kɛniɑ. Adɑmɑ u ǹ kɑ̃kɑ u Eli

bba	Filisitibɑ bɑ Gusunɔn woodɑn

bba	yi kpuro tɔn be tusiɑ.
bba	Sɑmuɛli u Sɔɔlu wisɑ u nɛɛ,
bba	nɛnɑ yɑm wɑo wi. A nɑ su dɑ

bba	kpuro wisi, kpɑ n de ɑ doonɑ.

bba	bɛɛ fɑɑbɑ kuɑ bɛɛn wɑhɑlɑ

bba	nɛɛ, u bɛɛ sunɔ kuo, u bɛɛ

bba	bweseru kɑ bweseru, kpɑ i tii tusiɑ
bba	yɛnu kɑ yɛnu win wuswɑɑɔ.
bba	Bɑ nɛɛ, ɑ ǹ sun tɑki diire, ɑ

bba	ǹ mɑɑ bɛsɛn ɡoon kɛ̃ru

bba	11-12 Sɑɑ yerɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u win
bba	sɔmɔ Gɑdi sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, ɑ doo

bba	Ye Isirelibɑ kpuro bɑ nuɑ nɡe mɛ
bba	sinɑ boko u siri bɑ nùn nɑsiɑ.
bba	Domi bɑ wɑ mɑ Gusunɔwɑ u nùn

bba	Hunde koni bɑɑyere ye yɑ ɡesi
bba	wɛ̃siɑmɔ, yu Yinni Gusunɔ siɑro.
bba	Yen sɔ̃, i ko bɛɛn himbɑ kɑ
bba	bɛɛn kookoosun ɑre di i debu.
bba	Ben swɛɛ kɑ ben sɑnu sɑnusu ku rɑ
bba	Bwisi yi koo nun ɑlɑfiɑ wɛ̃, kpɑ
bba	ɑ n bɔri yɛndu mɔ wunɛn wɑ̃ɑrun
bba	Sɔ̃ɔsi te bɑ nun kuɑ mi, ɑ ku tu
bba	yɔ̃su. A tu nɛnuɔ kem kem, domi
bba	terɑ tɑ sɑ̃ɑ wunɛn wɑ̃ɑrun
bba	A de mu n wɑ̃ɑ wunɛ turon sɔ̃. A
bba	ku de ɡɑbu bu kɑ nun mu bɔnu ko.
bba	A n ye kpuro nɛni bɑɑdommɑ wunɛn
bba	ɡɔ̃ruɔ, kpɑ ɑ ye doke wĩirɔ
bba	U turɑre bwese bwesekɑ nubu
bba	duroruɡiɑ yɛ̃kɑ kpinu wɔllɔ.
bba	Ye bɑ rɑ kɑsu kpuro sɔɔ,
bba	À n tɔn yɑɑ kɑsikio ɡerusi, u koo
bba	nun tusi. Adɑmɑ ɑ̀ n bwisiɡii
bba	ɡerusi, u koo nun kĩɑ.
bba	Gemɡiin ɡɑri yi rɑ kɑ tɔn dɑbinu
bba	ɑrufɑɑni nɑɑwɛ, ɑdɑmɑ ɡɑri
bba	bɑkɑsu su rɑ ɡbiwɑ sɛkum
bba	lɑɑkɑri sɑrirun sɔ̃.
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u tɔn kɔ̃sobu tusɑ,
bba	ɑdɑmɑ bèn sɑnu sɑnusu dɛɛre,
bba	berɑ u rɑ kɑ nɔnu ɡeu mɛɛri.
bba	Be bɑ rɑ kɔ̃sɑ bwisiku, weesɑ su
bba	rɑ n yibɑ ben ɡɔ̃ruɔ, ɑdɑmɑ be
bba	bɑ rɑ tɔmbu bwisi kɛ̃ bu kɑ ɡeɑ
bba	ko, bɑ rɑ n nuku dobu mɔwɑ.
bba	Sɑ̃ɑrobu bɑ rɑ dĩɑ ɡeenu wɑ
bba	ben ɡberun di, ɑdɑmɑ ɡɑbuɡiɑ
bba	rɑ ɡberewɑ yèn sɔ̃ bɑ ǹ ɡem
bba	Wi u ku rɑ mɔru ko fuuku, bwisi
bba	bɛkɛyɑ u mɔ, ɑdɑmɑ wìn mɔru
bba	yɑ rɑ se fuuku, ɡɑri bɑkɑrɑ u
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u rɑ tii suon diru
bba	surewɑ, ɑdɑmɑ u ku rɑ de bu
bba	ɡɔminin tem kɔɔrɔ mure.
bba	Be bɑ bwisi mɔ bɑ rɑ ɡɑri kowɑ
bba	kɑ lɑɑkɑri, kpɑ ben ɡɑri yi, yi
bba	Wi u ɡɑri bɔkɔ mɑrɑ, nuku
bba	sɑnkirɑnɑ u rɑ n mɔ. Mɛyɑ bii wi
bba	u kun ɑsɑnsi mɔn tundo u ǹ kpɛ̃
bba	Bɔrɔ dɑbinu nu koo kpĩ nu kɑ tɔnu
bba	nɔni swɑ̃ɑru nɑɑwɑ, ɑdɑmɑ
bba	bɔrɔ ɡoo u mɛro bisi kere.
bba	Sunɔn mɔru yɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ nɡe ɡbee
bba	sunɔn kukiribu. Bɑɑwure wi u nùn
bba	nɔɔ kuurimɔ, u win tii dokemɔwɑ
bba	Wi u sĩimɔ dee dee, win dɑɑ yɑ
bba	yɑ̃kuru kere Yinni Gusunɔn mi.
bba	Wi u lɑɑkɑri mɔ wiyɑ rɑ ɡbi u
bba	kɔ̃sɑ wɑ kpɑ u kuke, ɑdɑmɑ
bba	lɑɑkɑri sɑriruɡii u rɑ de u ye
bba	wɔriwɑ kpɑ u yen wɑhɑlɑ wɑ.
bba	Gobi yi rɑ doonɛwɑ sɑɑ ye kɑɑ
bba	nɛɛ, kɑɑ yi mɛɛri. N dɑ n
bba	sɑ̃ɑwɑ nɡe yi kɑsɑ mɔ yi kɑ
bba	yɔ̃ɔwɑ nɡe ɡunɔ bɑkeru.
bba	A ku tɔn kɔ̃sobun wɑ̃ɑru binɛ
bba	ko. A ku kĩɑ ɑ n kɑ bu wɑ̃ɑ.
bba	Mɑ nɑ ye mɛɛrɑ kɑ lɑɑkɑri,
bba	yerɑ nɑ bwisi dɔbɑ mi.
bba	Bɛɛrɛ ye bɑ ɡɑri bɔkɔ
bba	wɛ̃ɛmɔ, yɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ nɡe
bba	ɡbeburu wuburun sɑɑ sɔɔ, ǹ kun
bba	mɛ ɡurɑ ye yɑ nɛmɔ ɡɛ̃ɛbun
bba	Gerusibu bu kĩru kere te tɑ ǹ
bba	Wi u yinɑ u Gusunɔn woodɑ swɑɑ
bba	dɑki, Gusunɔ u rɑ yɛ̃ro yinɛwɑ
bba	Sinɑ boko ù n dɑ weesu swɑɑ dɑki,
bba	win sinɑ bwɑ̃ɑbu bɑ koo kowɑ tɔn
bba	Niyɑ, ɑ ku de nɑ n sɑ̃ɑ wee kowo,
bba	kpɑ n ku tɔmbu nɔni wɔ̃ke. A ku
bba	mɑɑ de nɑ n sɑ̃ɑ sɑ̃ɑro ǹ
bba	kun mɛ ɡobiɡii. A ɡesi mɑn
bba	wɛ̃ɛyɔ ye kon di nɑ n kɑ wɑ̃ɑ.
bba	ɡbee sunɔ ɡe ɡɑ yɛɛ kpuro bwisi
bba	Dɑm kɑ bɛɛrɛwɑ u rɑ n sebuɑ
bba	nɡe yɑberu. U ku rɑ wurure siɑn
bba	Nɑ yoo tɔn durɔbu kɑ tɔn kurɔbu
bba	dwɑ. Mɑ nɑ ben bii be bɑ mɑrɑ yoo
bba	te sɔɔ nɛni. Mɛyɑ nɑ mɑɑ kɛtɛ
bba	ɡɔ̃su kɑ yɑ̃ɑ ɡɔ̃su mɔ n
bba	kere sinɑm be bɑ mɑn ɡbiiye
bba	yɛ̃ɛsu mɑɑ kɑ sin sɑɑ.
bba	Wɑrɑ koo kpĩ u nɛɛ, tɔnun
bba	hundewɑ yɑ rɑ yɔ wɔllɔ kpɑ
bba	yɛɛɡiɑ yɑ n wɑ̃ɑ temɔ.
bba	Dukiɑ ye, yɑ rɑ kɑm kowɑ wɑhɑlɑ
bba	ɡɑɑ sɔɔ kpɑ u kun mɑɑ
bba	ɡɑ̃ɑnu mɔ sɑnɑm mɛ u bii mɑrɑ.
bba	A Gusunɔn nɔmɑn sɔmɑ mɛɛrio. Ye
bba	u derɑ yɑ sikire, wɑrɑ u koo kpĩ u
bba	Sɑnɑm mɛ nɑ tii wɛ̃ kɑ nɛn
bba	ɡɔ̃ru kpuro n kɑ bwisin sɑriɑ
bba	ɡiɑ, kpɑ n wɑ ye n koorɑmɔ
bba	hɑnduniɑ ye sɔɔ, nɑ wɑ bɑɑ mɛ
bba	tɔmbɑ ku rɑ dweeye sɔ̃ɔ sɔɔ kɑ
bba	wɔ̃kuru, bɑ ǹ kpɛ̃ bu tubu ye
bba	Gusunɔ u mɔ̀ kpuro hɑnduniɑ sɔɔ.
bba	Bwisiɡiin ɡɑri yi rɑ n bɛɛrɛ
bba	mɔ. Adɑmɑ ɡɑri bɔkɔn ɡɑri yi
bba	Yen sɔ̃, su ɡɑri yi kpuron wii
bba	ɡoberu swɑɑ dɑki te tɑ nɛɛ, ɑ
bba	Gusunɔ nɑsio kpɑ ɑ win woodɑbɑ
bba	mɛm nɔɔwɑ. Yerɑ, n weenɛ
bba	Wunɛn wĩirɑ kɑ ɡoonu wɑ̃.
bba	nɑ nɛn kĩnɑsin nɔɔ nɔɔmɔ.
bba	Ǹ n mɛn nɑ, kon sewɑ n bɔsu wuu
bba	Nu mɑɑ nɔɔ nɛwɑ swɛɛ swɛɛ,
bba	Wunɛ ɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ nɡe dɑ̃ɑ
bba	Nɑ nùn kɑsu kɑsu, nɑ ǹ nùn wɑ.
bba	mi turɑre bii wɑ̃ɑ yi yi kpiibu wee,
bba	Nɑ ǹ kɑ bɑɑru nɛn bwɛ̃rɑ mɑn
bba	Nɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ nɛn kĩnɑsiɡii,
bba	Mɛyɑ mɑɑ dɑɑnun nim yiburu tɑ
bba	ǹ kpɛ̃ tu kĩi te wukiri.
bba	nɡe wuu ɡe bɑ tɑbu bure bɑ doonɑ.
bba	Wee ɑ kuɑ nɡe sii bisu.
bba	su koo de i sekuru wɑ.
bba	mɛ Yinni Gusunɔ u sun wɛ̃ɛmɔ.
bba	ɡɑ̃ɑnu kpuro ɡesi ye bɑ kĩru bo.
bba	Yen sɔ̃, ɑ koowo bɛsɛn yɛnu
bba	mɑ i ye i sɑ̃ɑrobu mwɑɑri yii
bba	kpɑ ɑ de sɑ n wunɛn yĩsiru
bba	wɔllu kɑ tem Yinnin resɛm ɡbɑɑ te.
bba	Sɑɑ ye sɔɔ, tɔmbu kpurowɑ bɑ koo
bba	Yen sɔ̃nɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u koo de bu
bba	kpɑ wɔllu tu tĩrɑ ɡuru wii
bba	Mɑ u mɑn wisɑ u nɛɛ,
bba	Wee tɛ̃ win tii u koo bɛɛ yĩreru
bba	wɛ̃. Wɔndiɑ ɡoo u koo ɡurɑ suɑ
bba	kpɑ u bii tɔn durɔ mɑ, kpɑ u nùn
bba	yĩsiru kɛ̃ Emɑnuɛli.
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u mɑn sɔ̃ɔwɑ u
bba	nɛɛ, n seewo n yĩsi teni yore
bba	kpɑsɑsɑ, kpee bɛsi bɑkɑ ɡɑɑ
bba	sɔɔ, Mɑhɛɛ Sɑlɑli Hɑsibɑsi.
bba	Yen tubusiɑnɑ, bu seewo fuuku bu
bba	ɑrumɑni kpuro kɑtɑ ko bu ɡurɑ.
bba	Tɔn be bɑ rɑɑ sĩimɔ yɑm
bba	Tɔmbu kpuro, Efɑrɑimubɑ kɑ
bba	U koo bu nɔmu dokewɑ u sɛɛyɑsiɑ.
bba	bɔ̃rurobɑ bɛɛ Asiriɡibu.
bba	I ǹ mɑɑ suɡu dokemɔ
bba	ǹ kun mɛ, bɑ nɛɛn sɔ̃.
bba	be bɑ yɑrinɛ bɑ wɑ̃ɑ Asiriɔ kɑ
bba	Domi wunɑ ɑ sɑ̃ɑ bɛsɛn dɑm,
bba	be bɑ tɑbun sɔɔru kpɑ.
bba	yen sinɑ kpɑɑ burɑnu sɔɔ.
bba	wee ye kpuro yɑ wɔri ɡɔribun
bba	Bɑ ǹ mɑɑ wunɛn bwese kɔ̃surun
bba	Bɛɛ Filisitibɑ kpuro ɡesi i diirio,
bba	kpuro sɔɔ, wuri nɔɔrɑmɔ.
bba	kɑ ben woo bɔbunu kɑ ben ɡɑri kɑm
bba	Siriɡii be bɑ tie, bɑ ǹ Isirelibɑ
bba	Adɑmɑ Yinni Gusunɔ u bu ɡerusi,
bba	Sɑɑ ye sɔɔ, tɔn be bɑ ɡunu mi,
bba	mɑ ben wɑsi bɑllimɔ bɑ bu nɑsie
bba	bɑɑmɑ kpuro yèn sɔ̃ bɑ rɑ kpuro
bba	kɔsuku, mɑ dɑɑnu ben tem burɑnɛ,
bba	tɔn be, bɑ koo kɑ Gusunɔ wɔllu kɑ
bba	tem Yinni kɛ̃nu nɑɑwɑ Siɔnin
bba	ɡuurɔ mi bɑ rɑ nùn sɑ̃.
bba	Be bɑ sɑ̃ɑ tem mɛn dɑm bɑ koo
bba	wee nɛn sɔm kowo Esɑi u yɔ̃rɑ
bba	bɑsi mɑ u kɑ nɑɑ dirisu sĩɑ n
bba	kɑ kuɑ wɔ̃ɔ itɑ. Yeni yɑ
bba	sɑ̃ɑwɑ yĩreru te tɑ sɔ̃ɔsimɔ
bba	ye yɑ koo Eɡibitiɡibu kɑ
bba	Mɑ u ye kpuro mɛɛrɑ kɑ lɑɑkɑri.
bba	Wunɛn tɔn be bɑ mɛɛrɑ kuɑ, bɑ
bba	ǹ bu mɛɛrɑ kue tɑbu sɔɔ,
bba	Adɑmɑ i ǹ Gusunɔ mɛɛrɑ
bba	Ù n kɛniɑ, ɡoo kun kɛnumɔ.
bba	Yèn tɔmbu bɑ dɑ bɑ tem tukumɡibu
bba	kpɑ bu wunɛn ɡɑri yɑɑyɑ.
bba	domi yibɛrɛbɑ bɑ hɑniɑ mɔ̀ bɑ
bba	Bɑ ǹ mɑɑ nu seeyɑmɔ sere kɑ
bba	U koo ɡbɑ̃rɑ dɑmɡii ni nu ɡunu
bba	bɑ rɑ ɡiewɑ nɡe mɛ bɑ koo kɑ
bba	Nɛɡibu, bɛɛn tɔn be bɑ rɑɑ ɡu
bba	bu kɛri ko nɡe dɑ̃ɑ,
bba	Kpɑ bu yiirɑ bu Yinni Gusunɔ sɑ̃
bba	mɑ n kun mɔ bii wi bɑ bɔm kɑrɑ.
bba	Guru kpenu nu koo wee si kpuro kɔsuku
bba	U nùn yen kpunɑɑ sɔ̃ɔsi.
bba	kɑ ɡuru woo bɔkɔ, kɑ sere mɑɑ
bba	Kpɑ ben bwisiɡibun bwisi yi kpe.
bba	nɑ win debubu Isirelin yɛnuɡibu
bba	mi nuku sɑnkirɑrɑ wɑ̃ɑ.
bba	mɑ tɑ sɑ̃ɑ nɡe yɑrukɑ ben nɔsɔ
bba	Mɛyɑ mɑɑ ben dumi yi ǹ dɑm tukum
bba	kpɑ i kĩɑsu dewe nuku sɑnkirɑnun
bba	be, be bɑ dɑbi nɡe dɑ̃ɑ sɔ̃ɔ,
bba	Be bɑ ɡɔrɑ bu kɑ yibɛrɛbɑ suuru
bba	u ku rɑ tɔn ɡowobun ɡɑri swɑɑ
bba	Yinni Gusunɔwɑ u ko n sɑ̃ɑ bɛsɛn
bba	Edɔmun nim mu koo ɡɔsirɑ kontɑɑ.
bba	Wiyɑ u tem mɛ yĩirɑ,
bba	Nim mu koo yɑri mu koku
bba	I ku wurɑ i Yinni Gusunɔ nɑɑnɛ ko,
bba	bɑɑ Esekiɑsi ù n nɛɛ, Yinni
bba	Gusunɔ wi, u koo bɛɛ wɔrɑ. Yen
bba	sɔ̃nɑ n ǹ koorɔ Asirin sinɑ boko
bba	u koo win wɛ̃ru yɑbɑ u yɔni doke,
bba	nɡe yɑ̃ɑ kpɑron kuu bekuruɡiru.
bba	wɑ̃ɑ yerɑ tɑ koo nun siɑrɑ.
bba	nu ko nɡe tem tɛɛrɑ kpɑ swɛɛ yi
bba	Wɑrɑ u koo kpĩ u kɑ win niki binu
bba	wi, wi u wɑ̃ɑ wɔllɔ u tɔmbu
bba	Aluwɑɑsibɑ bɑ rɑ mɑɑ kpɑnɛ.

bba	Mɛyɑ nɑ ǹ mɑɑ nɛn bɛɛrɛ
bba	wɑrɑ u koo yeni swɑɑ dɑki bɛɛ
bba	n kɑ wunɛn wɑ̃ɑru yɑkiɑ.
bba	Mɑ nɑ nun fɑɑbɑ kuɑ.
bba	Domi kon de nim mu n wɑ̃ɑ
bba	ɡbɑburɔ, mi tem ɡbere,
bba	kpɑ u sɔ̃ɔsi nɡe mɛ nɑ kɑ
bba	hɑnduniɑ tɑkɑ kuɑ sɑɑ yellun di,
bba	Yerɑ sɛduru, ǹ kun mɛ sipɛrɛ,
bba	Ten sukum mɛ mu tie, mɑ u kɑ
bba	Adɑmɑ nɑ rɑ nɛn sɔm kowon ɡɑri
bba	U koo nɛn wuu Yerusɑlɛmun bɑnsu
bba	Gem ɡɑriyɑ u rɑ mɑɑ kpɑre.
bba	ɑdɑmɑ tɛ̃, nu kuɑ kubɑ ni yɑɑ
bba	Goo mɑɑ sɑri nɡe nɛ.
bba	Nɛn yĩsirɑ Gusunɔ, wɔllu
bba	Wunɛn lɑɑkɑri kɑ wunɛn yɛ̃ru
bba	mɑ i tɑ̃sɑ nɛ Gusunɔ, Isirelibɑn
bba	Mɑ nɑ nɛn tii nɛnuɑ nɛn yiikon
bba	Wee, tɛ̃ Yinni Gusunɔ u mɑn
bba	ɡɔrimɑ kɑ win Hunde.
bba	Ten min diyɑ u koo win yiiko sɔ̃ɔsi.
bba	mɛ mu bɑnsu sɑ̃ɑ tɛ̃.
bba	Kpɑ be bɑ rɑɑ nun wɔri
bba	Be bɑ mɑɑ mɑn yĩiyɔ bɑ ǹ
bba	Nɑ rɑ de wɔllu tu yɑm tĩrɑ,
bba	Bɛɛ be i mɔru seewɑ nɡe dɔ̃ɔ,
bba	Mɛn tɔmbu bɑ koo ɡbi nɡe sɔnsu.
bba	be, be bɑ kɑsu bu bɛɛ kpeerɑsiɑ.
bba	nɡe nɛm ni bɑ tɑɑ mwɑ.
bba	Wee, be bɑ rɑ ɡbɑ̃rɑru kɔ̃su
bba	Mɑ Esɑi u wisɑ u nɛɛ,
bba	ǹ kun mɛ, yɑ̃ɑ te tɑ mɑɑri
bba	kɑɑ bibu mɑ bɑ n dɑbi,
bba	Nɛ wi nɑ nun yɑkiɑmɔ, nɛnɑ nɑ
bba	Nɛ, Gusunɔ wunɛn Yinnin sɔ̃,
bba	kpɑ ye kpuro yu ko yĩreru
bba	be kpuro be bɑ tɔ̃ɔ wɛ̃rɑruɡiru
bba	ɡoo ku rɑ bu weeweenu kue.
bba	i bɛɛn bũu wi bɑ mɔ̀ Mɔlɔku
bba	wi bɑ tɑɑre mɑ win nuki sɑnkire,
bba	Tɔ̃ɔ bɑɑtere bɑ rɑ n mɑn sokuwɑ
bba	I bɛɛn dĩɑnu bɔnu koowo
bba	kpɑ bu de tɔmbu bɑ n wɑ̃ɑ mi
bba	N ǹ mɔ yi wɑ̃ɑ yi kɑ ɡɑ̃ɑ
bba	ɑdɑmɑ wunɛn fɑɑbɑ yɑ kɑ sun
bba	kpɑ bu win yĩsiru nɑsiɑ
bba	bɑ n wurɑ kɑ turɑre sɔɔwɑ,
bba	kpɑ bu kɑ nɛn sɑ̃ɑ yeru burɑru
bba	N ǹ mɑɑ sɔ̃ɔ u koo nun yɑm

bba	Bwesenu kpuro nu koo be kɑ ben
bba	Bɑ koo mu sokuwɑ kurɔ kpɑo,
bba	kɑ ben tɔn be bɑ rɑɑ yoru
bba	win wɔnwɔndu kɑ win kĩi bɑkɑrun
bba	kpɑ ɑ wɑ ye yɑ sun mɔ̀.
bba	Wunɛ bɑɑsi, sɑ ǹ mɑɑ ɡoo
bba	Gɑ̃ɑ ɡee ni sɑ mɑɑ mɔ kpuro, nu
bba	Kon bɛɛ bɛɛn kookoo si i kuɑn ɑre
bba	bɑ koo womusu ko kɑ nuku dobu.
bba	bɑ koo nɛɛwɑ, nɑ yɛ̃ro bɔ̃rusi.
bba	Adɑmɑ nɛn tɔmbun sɑ̃ɑru tɑ ǹ
bba	U ǹ mɑrubun wɑhɑlɑ wɑ, u kɑ bii
bba	Wee, nɑ sisi nɑ wɑ̃ɑ dɔ̃ɔ
bba	Sɔ̃ɔ teeru Yinni Gusunɔ u kɑ nɛ,

bba	nɛɛ, wee Filisitibɑ bɑ Isirelibɑ
bba	mɔru kɔsie kɑ dɑm domi bɑ
bba	sɑ̃ɑwɑ ben yibɛrɛbɑ sɑɑ yellun
bba	Esekiɛli u nɛɛ, Tiri, Yinni Gusunɔ
bba	Toɡɑɑmɑɡibu bɑ rɑ mɑɑ dumi yi
bba	bɑ rɑ kɑ sɔmburu ko kɑ yi bɑ rɑ
bba	kɑ tɑbu de kɑ kɛtɛkunu dɔrɑm nɛ
bba	bu nun ɡɔɔ swĩiyɑ nuku
bba	Win tenkurun kpɑ̃ɑru tɑ derɑ u
bba	bɔbunu kɑ keetɑ wɔri. Yen sɔ̃,
bba	kon nùn surɑ sɑɑ nɛn ɡuu dɛɛrɑ
bba	ten min di, wi, wi u sɑ̃ɑ nɡe
bba	wɔllun kɔ̃so mi. Kon de u doonɑ
bba	sɑɑ kpee ni nu bɑllimɔ min suunu
bba	Yen sɔ̃nɑ nɛ, Yinni Gusunɔ nɑ
bba	nɛɛ, kon Bɑbilonin sinɑ boko
bba	Eɡibitin dukiɑ kpuro wɛ̃. U koo ben
bba	yɑ̃nu ɡurɑ kpɑ nu n sɑ̃ɑ win
bba	tɑbu kowobun kɔsiɑru.
bba	Wee u sɑ̃ɑwɑ nɡe Libɑnin dɑ̃ɑ
bba	Edɛnin ɡbɑɑ te sɔɔ, dɑ̃ɑ
bba	ɡɑɑ kun kɑ Eɡibitin sinɑ boko nɛ
bba	burɑm sɔɔ kɑ kpɑ̃ɑru sɔɔ. Kɑ
bba	mɛ, bɑ koo nùn surewɑ ɡɔribun
bba	wɑ̃ɑ yerɔ tem sɔɔ sɔɔwɔ kɑ
bba	dɑ̃ɑ ni nu wɑ̃ɑ Edɛni mi sɑnnu
bba	kpɑ u n kpĩ kɑ be bɑ ɡo tɑbu
bba	sɔɔ kɑ tɑkobi, be bɑ ǹ Gusunɔ
bba	yɛ̃n suunu sɔɔ. Yeniwɑ yɑ koo
bba	Eɡibitin sinɑ boko kɑ win tɔn dɑbi
bba	te kpuro deemɑ. Nɛ, Yinni Gusunɔwɑ
bba	nɑ yeni kpuro ɡeruɑ.
bba	Mɛsɛki kɑ Tubɑli bɑ kpĩ kɑ ben
bba	tɑbu kowobu kpuro. Mɑ tɑbu kowo ben
bba	sikɑ beɡiɑ sikerenɛ. Be, be bɑ ǹ
bba	Gusunɔ yɛ̃ mi, bɑ ɡuwɑ tɑbu
bba	sɔɔ. Beyɑ tɔmbɑ rɑɑ nɑsie.
bba	Yen sɔ̃, ɑ bu sɔ̃ɔwɔ ɑ nɛɛ,
bba	wee ye nɛ, Yinni Gusunɔ nɑ bu
bba	sɔ̃ɔmɔ. Nɑ nɛɛ, bɑ yɑɑ temmɔ
bba	kɑ yen yɛm sɑnnu. Bɑ bũnu
bba	sɑ̃ɑmɔ, mɑ bɑ tɔmbu ɡoomɔ.
bba	Yerɑ bɑ tɑmɑɑ tem mɛ, mu ko n
bba	Kon nu kpɑro turo wɛ̃ wi u koo nu
bba	nɔɔri. U koo yɑriwɑ nɛn sɔm kowo
bba	Dɑfidin bweserun di. U koo nu nɔɔri
bba	kpɑ u n sɑ̃ɑ nin kpɑro ɡeo.
bba	Sɑɑ ye sɔɔ, bɛɛ ɡuunun dɑ̃nu i
bba	ko kpɑrɑ kpɑ i binu mɑ win tɔmbu
bba	Isirelibɑn sɔ̃. Domi ben wurɑmɑru
bba	Yinni Gusunɔn dɑm mu Esekiɛli
bba	nɛnuɑ mɑ mu win bwɛ̃rɑ suɑ mu
bba	kɑ dɑ wɔwɑ ɡɑɑn suunu sɔɔ.
bba	Wɔwɑ ye sɔɔ, kukunɑ nu yibɑ.
bba	wee ye nɛ, Yinni Gusunɔ nɑ ɡerumɔ.
bba	Nɑ nɛɛ, kon Gɔɡu wɔrimɑ wi u
bba	sɑ̃ɑ Mɛsɛki kɑ Tubɑlin kpɑro.
bba	Yen tɔ̃ɔ te, Isireliɔ kon Gɔɡu
bba	siku yeru wɛ̃ nim wɔ̃ku bɔruɡuun
bba	sɔ̃ɔ yɑri yeru ɡiɑ, mi tɔmbɑ
bba	rɑ sɑre. Kpɑ tu berɑ min swɑɑ
bba	ɡo. Miyɑ bɑ koo Gɔɡu kɑ win tɔn
bba	dɑbi te sike, kpɑ bu yɑm mi soku
bba	Gɔɡun tɔn dɑbinun wɔwɑ.
bba	U mɑɑ dii sɔɔ ɡe yĩirɑ mɑ ɡɑ
bba	kuɑ ɡɔm soonu yɛndu. Dii ten berɑ
bba	ɡiɑ, sɑ̃ɑ yee ten yɑɑrɑ yɑ kɑ
bba	kɔnnɔ ɡe sikerenɛwɑ.
bba	U mɑn sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, dii tèn
bba	kɔnnɔ ɡɑ tĩi sɔ̃ɔ yɛ̃sɑn
bba	nɔm dwɑru ɡiɑ mi, tɑ sɑ̃ɑwɑ
bba	yɑ̃ku kowobun diru be bɑ rɑ sɑ̃ɑ
bba	Bɑ ɡɑmbo yen wɔllɔ wɔllun
bba	kɔ̃sobun weenɑsibu kɑ kpɑkpɑ
bba	wurusun weenɑsisu kuɑ nɡe mɛ bɑ
bba	kuɑ ɡɑni yi sɔɔ. Mɑ bɑ kɔbɛ

bba	Tɛ̃ ben bũu ɡɑsiribu bu koo nɔru

bba	ɡɑri duɑri. Kpɑ nɑ n wɑ̃ɑ ben
bba	suunu sɔɔ sere kɑ bɑɑdommɑɔ.
bba	Nɑ ǹ mɑɑ wurɑmɔ bu mɑn susi bu
bba	Isirelibɑ yɑ̃kuru kuɑ. Bɑ ǹ
bba	mɑɑ duɔ nɛn sɑ̃ɑ yerun dii
bba	dɛɛrɑrɔ kɑ dii te tɑ dɛɛre ɡem

bba	Wee kɛ̃ɛ ni i ko i n dɑ wɛ̃. Ì

bba	ɡeu ɡiɑn di. Yen sɔɔ mi, ɑyeru
bba	ɡɑrɑ wɑ̃ɑ sɔ̃ɔ duu yeru ɡiɑ.

bba	ɑsɑkpɔbun ɡɑri yi nuɑ. Yerɑ u

bba	bɑkɑru dimɔ. U nɛɛ, sinɑ boko,
bba	wunɛn hunde yu dɑkɑɑ dɑ! A ku

bba	Sɑɑ ye Dɑniɛli u nuɑ mɑ bɑ

bba	kɑ mɛ, dɔ̃ɔ u koo nɑ u bɛɛ di,

bba	yen ɡɑɑ kun kpɛ̃ yu bu wɔrɑ

bba	Bɛɛ Isirelibɑ kpuro ɡesi, i nuku
bba	Wi, Yinni Gusunɔwɑ u yeni ɡeruɑ.
bba	Yerɑ Asee u mɑɑ nɛɛ, ɑmɛniwɑ
bba	Yinni Gusunɔ u ɡeruɑ u nɛɛ, nɡe

bba	kpee kpikiru. Bɑ ǹ nɛ, Gusunɔ

bba	sɔmɔbun min di, be nɛn Hunde u kɑ
bba	ɡɑri kuɑ. Mɑ ben swɑɑ tɑɑ bi,

bba	Nɛn bɔrɔbɑrɑ bɛɛ i sɑ̃ɑ ì n
bba	mɔ̀ ye nɑ bɛɛ yiire.
bba	Mɑ win bwɑ̃ɑbu ɡɑbu bɑ
bba	bikiɑnɑmɔ, mbɑ yen tubusiɑnu ye u
bba	sun sɔ̃ɔmɔ, ǹ n sosi fiiko sɑ ǹ
bba	mɑɑ nùn wɑsi, ǹ n mɑɑ kpɑm sosi
bba	fiiko sɑ ko nùn wɑ. Mbɑ mɑɑ yen
bba	tubusiɑnu ye u nɛɛ u dɔɔ win
bba	Nɑ ǹ nun kɑnɑmɔ ɑ kɑ bu wunɑ
bba	hɑnduniɑ sɔɔn di, ɑdɑmɑ nɑ nun
bba	kɑnɑmɔwɑ ɑ bu kɔ̃suo tɔn
bba	Mɑ wɔndiɑ wi u kɔnnɔ kɔ̃su mi, u
bba	Piɛɛ bikiɑ u nɛɛ, wunɛ, ɑ ǹ
bba	mɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ durɔ win bwɑ̃ɑbun
bba	Mɑ tɑbu kowobu bɑ sɑ̃ki tundu
bba	bɔkɑnɑ bɑ kɑ nùn sinɑ furɔ kuɑ
bba	bɑ doke win wirɔ. Bɑ mɑɑ nùn
bba	ɡurumusu swɑ̃ɑbu sebusiɑ.
bba	Mɑ bɑ nɛn yɑberu tɛtɛ toosi.”
bba	Mɑ bwɑ̃ɑ be, bɑ ɡɔsirɑ bɑ dɑ
bba	Ye yɑm sɑ̃rɔ Yesu u yɔ̃ dɑɑrun
bba	ɡoorɔ, ɑdɑmɑ bwɑ̃ɑ be, bɑ ǹ

bba	kpuro sɔɔ bu yen ɑyeru wɑ mi bɑ
bba	koo tire ni kpuro doke ni bɑ koo rɑ
bba	Bin biru bɑ ɡɑ̃ɑnu wɑ nɡe
bba	dɔ̃ɔ yɑri yi tɛriɑ, mɑ yi sinɑ
bba	I ɡɑri yi swɑɑ dɑkio, bɛɛ
bba	Isirelibɑ. Yesu Nɑsɑrɛtiɡiin
bba	ɡɑriyɑ nɑ bɛɛ sɔ̃ɔmɔ, wi
bba	Gusunɔ u bɛɛ ɡiɑsiɑ sɔm
bba	mɑɑmɑɑkiɡiɑ ye u kuɑ bɛɛn
bba	suunu sɔɔ, sɑɑ win min di nɡe mɛ
bba	Nɑɑnɛ dokeobu kpuro bɑ wɑ̃ɑ

bba	Bɑ mɔru bɑrɑ yèn sɔ̃ ɡɔro be,
bba	bɑ tɔmbu keu sɔ̃ɔsimɔ bɑ Yesun

bba	kɔnnɔwɔ. Adɑmɑ ye sɑ ɡɑmbobɑ

bba	ɡɑɡu nuɑ ɡɑ nɛɛ, Sɔɔlu,
bba	Sɔɔlu, mbɑn sɔ̃nɑ ɑ mɑn nɔni
bba	Piɛɛ u mɑɑ bɔsu bɑɑmɑ kpuro.

bba	ɡɑbɑ wɑ̃ɑ Antiɔsin Yesun

bba	Bɑ nɛɛ, Yohɑnun bɑtɛmu.

bba	tii kuɑ sɑ̃ɑro bɛɛn sɔ̃ kpɑ
bba	win sɑ̃ɑ te, tu kɑ bɛɛ ko
bba	U ko n dɑ bɛɛ dukiɑ wɛ̃ ye yɑ
bba	koo turi i kɑ kɛ̃ru wɛ̃
bba	bɑɑdommɑ kɑ nuku tiɑ. Tɔn dɑbinu
bba	koo mɑɑ Gusunɔ siɑrɑ bɛɛn
bba	Sɑnɑm mɛ nɑ wɑ̃ɑ bɛɛn mi,
bba	nɑ̀ n ɡɑ̃ɑnun bukɑtɑ mɔ, n ku
bba	rɑ kɑ ko bɛɛn ɡoon sɔmunu, domi
bba	bɛsɛɡii be bɑ nɑ Mɑsedɔnin di
bba	bɑ kɑ mɑn ye kpuro nɑɑwɑ yèn
bba	bukɑtɑ nɑ mɔ. Nɑ tii nɛnuɑ kpuro
bba	sɔɔ kpɑ nɑ kun sɑ̃ɑ bɛɛn
bba	sɔmunu. Mɛyɑ ko nɑ n mɑɑ tii
bba	Bɑɑ nɑ̀ n woo kɑnɑbu kĩ, nɑ ǹ
bba	kon ko wiiro domi ɡeeyɑ kon ɡere.
bba	Adɑmɑ nɑ ǹ wurɑmɔ n woo kɑnɑ
bba	kpɑ ɡoo u ku rɑɑ mɑn mɛɛri n
bba	kere nɡe mɛ u mɑn wɑɑmɔ, ǹ kun
bba	mɛ, nɡe mɛ u nɔɔmɔ nɛn nɔɔn di.
bba	Nɛnɑ Pɔlu. Yesu Kirisiwɑ u mɑn
bba	sokɑ n kɑ ko win ɡɔro, wi kɑ
bba	Gusunɔ Bɑɑbɑ, wi u nùn seeyɑ
bba	ɡɔrin di. N ǹ mɔ tɔmbɑ bɑ mɑn
bba	sokɑ, nɛn sokurɑ kun nɛ sɑɑ tɔnu
bba	Gɑbu be Yɑkɔbu u ɡɔrɑ mi, bu sere
bba	tunumɑ, Piɛɛ u rɑ rɑɑ di kɑ tɔn
bba	tuko nɑɑnɛ dokeobu sɑnnu. Adɑmɑ
bba	ye tɔn be, bɑ tunumɑ bɑ kpɑ, u tii
bba	ɡɑwɑ mɑ u ǹ mɑɑ dimɔ kɑ be
bba	Adɑmɑ Gusunɔn ɡɑri ɡerumɔ mɑ
bba	tɔmbu kpuro bɑ wɑ̃ɑ durum dɑm
bba	nɔmɑɔ, kpɑ kɛ̃ɛ tèn nɔɔ
bba	mwɛɛru Gusunɔ u kuɑ tɑ n kɑ
bba	sɑ̃ɑ be bɑ nɑɑnɛ dokeɡiru yèn
bba	sɔ̃ bɑ Yesu Kirisi nɑɑnɛ doke.
bba	Gɑri yini yi kuɑ weesinɑɑ. Kurɔ be
bba	yiru bɑ kɑ nɔɔ mwɛɛnu yiru
bba	weenɛ. Teeru, te tɑ bibu mɑrumɔ
bba	yoru sɔɔ, tɑ nɑɑmɔ sɑɑ Sinɑin
bba	ɡuurun di, teyɑ tɑ kɑ Aɡɑɑ
bba	Tɔnun tii tiin dɑɑ yɑ rɑ
bba	sɔ̃ɔsire kpɑsɑsɑ. Yeyɑ kɔ̃ɔ
bba	mɛnnɑbu tɑntɑnɑru sɔɔ, kɑ dɑɑ
bba	disinuɡiɑ kɑ dɑɑ bɛrɛtɛkɛ,
bba	kpɑ su kɑ win durom yiikoɡim siɑrɑ
bba	mɛ u sun kuɑ bɛsɛ kɑ win Bii
bba	kĩnɑsin ɡbinnɑɑ sɔɔ.
bba	Kɑ win ɡɔɔwɑ u woodɑ kpeesiɑ kɑ
bba	yen yiirebu kɑ yen sesenu, kpɑ u kɑ
bba	kpĩ u bwesenu yiru ye ko bwese kpɑɑ
bba	teeru deɡe deɡe win tii sɔɔ. Nɡe
bba	mɛyɑ u kɑ bɔri yɛndu doke ben
bba	I hɑniɑ koowo i n kɑ nɔɔ tiɑ
bba	sɑ̃ɑ ye yɑ wee Hunde Dɛɛron min
bba	di kpɑ i n ɡbinnɛ bɔri yɛndu sɔɔ.
bba	I durom kuɑnɔ kpɑ i n wɔnwɔndu
bba	mɔɔsinɛ. I suuru kuɑnɔ nɡe mɛ
bba	Gusunɔ u bɛɛ suuru kuɑ Kirisin
bba	Mɛyɑ n weenɛ durɔbu bu ben kurɔbu
bba	kĩɑ nɡe mɛ bɑ ben tiin wɑsi kĩ.
bba	Wi u win kurɔ kĩ, u win tii kĩwɑ.
bba	Gusunɔ bɛsɛn Bɑɑbɑ kɑ Yinni Yesu
bba	Kirisi bu bɛɛ durom kuɑ kpɑ bu
bba	I ku ɡɑ̃ɑnu ko kinɛnun sɔ̃, ǹ
bba	kun mɛ tii suɑbun sɔ̃, ɑdɑmɑ i
bba	tii kɑwo kpɑ i wurɑ mɑ ɡɑbɑ
bba	I n tii sɛ kɑ kɔ̃sɑn kowobu be bɑ
bba	sɑ̃ɑ nɡe bɔ̃nu, mɑ bɑ wɑsin
bba	Nɑ yɑ̃ɑrun dɔɔnɛ mɔ, nɑ mɑɑ
bba	mɔɔ bɑkɑrun dɔɔnɛ mɔ. Yɑm
bba	kpuro kɑ ye n mɑn deemɑ kpuro sɔɔ,
bba	nɑ ɡiɑ mɛ kon ko deburun sɑɑ kɑ
bba	ɡɔ̃ɔrun sɑɑ. Nɑ mɑɑ yɛ̃ mɛ
bba	kon ko mɔɔ bɑkɑru sɔɔ kɑ
bba	Bɛɛ mɑɑ, i rɑɑ ɡɑsɔ kɑ
bba	Gusunɔ tomɑ, i rɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ win
bba	yibɛrɛbɑ bɛɛn bwisikunu sɔɔ
bba	bɛɛn kookoo kɔ̃susun sɔ̃.
bba	Geemɑ, woodɑ be, bɑ kɑ bwisin
bba	ɡɑ̃ɑnu weenɛ ɑ̀ n bu mɛɛrɑ,
bba	kɑ ben sɑ̃ɑru te tɑ wee sɑɑ

bba	kɑwɑ weesuɡibu, kɑ mɑɑ ben wɑsin
bba	seserun serusiɑbu. Adɑmɑ bɑɑ
bba	woodɑ ben tiɑ kun dɑm ɡɑm mɔ yu
bba	kɑ wɑsin kĩru kɑnkɑm tɑɑre.
bba	I de bɛɛn ɡɑri yi n nɔɔbu do kpɑ
bba	yi n swɑɑ swĩi, kpɑ i n kɑ yɛ̃
bba	nɡe mɛ n weenɛ i bɑɑwure wisi.
bba	Yèn sɔ̃ sɑ bɛɛ kĩ ɡem ɡem sɑ
bba	rɑɑ sɔɔru sɑ̃ɑ, n ǹ mɔ su kɑ
bba	bɛɛ Gusunɔn Lɑbɑɑri ɡeɑ wɛ̃
bba	tɔnɑ, ɑdɑmɑ kɑ mɑɑ bɛsɛn tiin
bba	wɑ̃ɑru, domi bɛɛn kĩrɑ sun nɛni.
bba	Domi Gusunɔ kun sun sokɑ su kɑ dɑɑ
bba	disinuɡiɑ ko mɑ n kun mɔ sɑ n
bba	I ku Gusunɔn sɔmɔbun ɡɑri ɡɛm.
bba	Nɡe mɛyɑ, be bɑ ǹ ɡem nɑɑnɛ
bba	doke mɑ bɑ kom kɔ̃sum kuɑ kɑ nuku
bba	dobu, bɑ koo tɑɑrɛ suɑ.
bba	Kpɑ u n yɛ̃ mɑ bɑ ǹ woodɑ kue
bba	ɡemɡibun sɔ̃. Bɑ ye kuɑwɑ woodɑ
bba	sɑrobu kɑ mɛm nɔɔ sɑriruɡibun
bba	sɔ̃, kɑ be bɑ ǹ Gusunɔn bɛɛrɛ
bba	yɛ̃, kɑ durumɡibu, kɑ mɑɑ tɔn
bba	be bɑ ǹ Gusunɔ kɑ ɡɑ̃ɑ
bba	dɛɛrɑnun bɛɛrɛ yɛ̃, kɑ sere be

bba	ɑmɔnɑ yɛ̃ro wi, u koo kɑ kpĩ u
bba	Gusunɔn yiɡbɛru nɛnɛ.

bba	nɛnɛ, kɑ mɑɑ sɔ̃ɔsi te tɑ
bba	Gusunɔn bɛɛrɛ wɛ̃ɛbu
bba	A nɛn sɔ̃ɔsiru nɛnuɔ kɑ nɑɑnɛ
bba	dokebu Yesu Kirisi sɔɔ kɑ kĩi te ɑ

bba	sɑriruɡisun di. A yɛ̃ kɑm kɑm mɑ
bba	siyɑ su rɑ sɑnnɔ mɑ.

bba	durɔbu wiru kpĩiyɑmmɛ, kpɑ ɡoo ku

bba	kpuro tubu ni sɑ mɔ Kirisin sɑɑbu.

bba	Wɑrɑ rɑ n tɔnu ɑ n sere kɑ nùn

bba	Ǹ n ben sɔ̃n nɑ, be bɑ rɑɑ yɑm

bba	ko tɔ̃ɔ wɛ̃rɑruɡiru sɔɔ.
bba	Tɔn ɡeo u rɑ ɡɑ̃ɑ ɡeenu
bba	yɑrewɑ ɡɑ̃ɑ ɡeenu sɔɔn di ni
bba	nu beruɑ win ɡɔ̃ruɔ. Tɔn kɔ̃so
bba	mɑɑ ɡɑ̃ɑ kɔ̃sunu yɑrɑmɔ
bba	ɡɑ̃ɑ kɔ̃sunu sɔɔn di ni nu
bba	I ko n mɛɛrimɔ ɑdɑmɑ i ǹ ko i
bba	Setɑmwɑ mɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ yibɛrɛ wi u
bba	su duurɑ. Gɛ̃ɛbun sɑɑ mɑɑ
bba	sɑ̃ɑ hɑnduniɑn kpeeru. Gusunɔn
bba	ɡɔrɑdobɑrɑ bɑ mɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ
bba	Mɑ Yohɑnun bwɑ̃ɑbɑ nɑ bɑ win
bba	ɡoru suɑ bɑ sikuɑ mɑ bɑ dɑ bɑ
bba	Adɑmɑ bɛɛ i ɡerumɔ mɑ ɡoo ù n
bba	win tundo ǹ kun mɛ win mɛro
bba	sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, win dukiɑ ye u koo
bba	kpĩ u kɑ nùn somi yɑ kuɑ
bba	Win bwɑ̃ɑbɑ nùn bikiɑ bɑ nɛɛ,
bba	mɑnɑ sɑ ko sere dĩɑnu wɑ
bba	ɡbɑburu sɔɔ mini ni nu koo tɔn
bba	Yen biru Yesu win bwɑ̃ɑbu sɔ̃ɔwɑ
bba	u nɛɛ, ɡoo ù n kĩ u mɑn swĩi
bba	nɡe bɔ̃̀ɔ, u win ɡɔ̃ru kĩru
bba	derio kpɑ u win tiin dɑ̃ɑ
bba	bunɑnɑru suɑ u n kɑ mɑn swĩi.
bba	Ye Piɛɛ u duɔ dirɔ Yesu ɡbiɑ u
bba	nùn bikiɑ u nɛɛ, ɑmɔnɑ ɑ wɑ
bba	Simɔɔ. Berɑ̀ n weenɛ bu hɑnduniɑ
bba	min sinɑmbu ɡbere ɡobi kɔsiɑ.
bba	Sinɑ bibu? Nɡe ɡɑbu.
bba	Ye sɔm kowo wi, u yɑrɑ min di, u kɑ
bba	win sɔm kowosi yinnɑ wi u win dibu
bba	nɛni nɡe fɔrɔtɔ nɔɔbun sɑkɑ.
bba	Yerɑ u nùn sɛ̃re u wĩiru sɛ̃kɑ
bba	u nɛɛ, ɑ nɛn dibu kɔsiɑmɑ bi ɑ
bba	Yerɑ Yesu u win bwɑ̃ɑbu sɔ̃ɔwɑ
bba	u nɛɛ, kɑ ɡeemɑ nɑ bɛɛ
bba	sɔ̃ɔmɔ, n sɛ̃ ɡem ɡem
bba	dukiɑɡii u kɑ bɑn te Gusunɔ u
bba	Mɑ bɑ nɛɛ, sɑ ko kpĩ.
bba	Yen biru u bu deri u doonɑ wuu min di
bba	u dɑ Betɑniɔ u kpunɑ mi.
bba	“Kpee te bɑnɔbɑ yinɑ, terɑ tɑ
bba	kuɑ ɡɑni ɡɔmburun dɑm.
bba	bɑ nɛɛ, tɔnwero, Mɔwisi nɛɛ,
bba	durɔ ɡoo ù n ɡu ù kun bii mɑrɑ,
bba	win wɔnɔwɑ koo win ɡɔmini yɛnu
bba	doke kpɑ u kɑ win mɔɔ bweseru
bba	Bɑ mɑɑ sin yee bɛɛrɛɡinu kĩ dii
bba	Mɑ Yesu u nɛɛ, Yerusɑlɛmu,
bba	Yerusɑlɛmu, wunɛ wi ɑ rɑ Gusunɔn
bba	sɔmɔbu ɡo kpɑ ɑ be u nun ɡɔriɑ
bba	kpenu kɑsuku. Nɔn nyewɑ nɑ kĩɑ n
bba	wunɛn tɔmbu kpɑɑsinɑ nɛn bɔkuɔ
bba	nɡe mɛ ɡoo mɛro ɡɑ rɑ ɡen binu
bba	mɛnnɛ ɡen kɑsɑ sɔɔ, ɑdɑmɑ i
bba	Mɑ Yesu mɑɑ nɛɛ, sɑnɑm mɛn
bba	nɔni swɑ̃ɑrun biru, mii mii sɔ̃ɔ
bba	koo yɑm tĩrɑ, suru kun mɑɑ win
bba	yɑm bururɑm sɔ̃ɔsimɔ, kperi koo
bba	wɔrumɑ wɔllun di kpɑ wɔllun dɑm
bba	Lɑɑkɑriɡii be, bɑ wisɑ bɑ nɛɛ,
bba	ɑɑwo domi n ǹ koo bɛsɛ kpuro
bba	turi. I yɑnde doo i bɛɛɡim dwe.
bba	Sunɔ u koo bu wisi u nɛɛ, kɑ
bba	ɡeemɑ nɑ bɛɛ sɔ̃ɔmɔ, mɛn nɔ
bba	i bwɛ̃ɛbwɛ̃ɛ benin turo ye kuɑ
bba	Tɔnun Bii u koo ɡbi nɡe mɛ Gusunɔn
bba	ɡɑri yi win ɡɑri mɔ̀, ɑdɑmɑ
bba	nɔni swɑ̃ɑruɡiiwɑ wi u koo nùn
bba	dɔmɛ. N burɑm bo bɑ kun dɑɑ
bba	Yesun tɔmbun turo u win tɑkobi womɑ,
bba	u kɑ yɑ̃ku kowo tɔnweron yoon soo
bba	U nɛɛ, nɑ durum kuɑ ye nɑ kɑ tɔn
bba	Bɑ nùn yɑ̃ɑtɑm siriki mɑ bɑ
bba	dɛkɑ wɛ̃ɛnɑ bɑ kɑ nùn soomɔ
bba	Mɑɑri Mɑdɑlɑɡii kɑ Mɑɑri
bba	wiɔnɔ bɑ sɔ̃ siki ten bɔkuɔ.
bba	Bɑɑ mɛ i ye kpuro yɛ̃ sɑ̃ɑ
bba	sɑ̃ɑ, kɑ mɛ, nɑ kĩ n bɛɛ
bba	yɑɑyɑsiɑ mɑ ye Yinni Gusunɔ u
bba	Isirelin tɔmbu wɔrɑ sɑɑ Eɡibitin
bba	tem di u kpɑ, yen biru u be bɑ ǹ
bba	nɑɑnɛ doke kɑm koosiɑ.
bba	ɡɑ nɛɛ, n yoruo tireru sɔɔ ye nɑ
bba	wɑɑmɔ, kpɑ n tire te mɔrisiɑ
bba	Yesun yiɡbɛnu nɔɔbɑ yirun mi,
bba	Efesuɔ, kɑ Simiiniɔ, kɑ
bba	Pɛɛɡɑmuɔ, kɑ Tiɑtirɑɔ, kɑ
bba	Sɑɑduɔ, kɑ Filɑdɛɛfiɔ, kɑ
bba	nɑ win kookoosu yɛ̃. Nɑ win kĩru
bba	yɛ̃, kɑ win bɔrɔkiniru, kɑ win
bba	tɔn ɡeeru kɑ mɑɑ win tɛmɑnɑbu.
bba	Nɑ yɛ̃ mɑ win sɔm dɑ̃ɑkiru tɑ
bba	Wi u swɑɑ mɔ u nɔɔwɔ ye Hunde
bba	Dɛɛro u Yesun yiɡbɛnu sɔ̃ɔmɔ.
bba	kpɑ ɑ yĩre ni kusiɑ.
bba	Kperi mɑɑ wɔrukumɔ temɔ nɡe mɛ
bba	ɡɑndun bii birenu rɑ dɛrure sɑnɑm
bba	mɛ woo dɑmɡuu ɡɑ tu sirɑmɔ.
bba	mɑ hunde konibɑ kpuro be bɑ wɑ̃ɑ
bba	nim wɔ̃ku sɔɔn bɔnu itɑse bɑ
bba	ɡu, ɡoo nimkusu kpuron bɔnu itɑse
bba	mɑ u bɔ̃ruɑ kɑ Gusunɔn yĩsiru wi
bba	u wɑ̃ɑ sere kɑ bɑɑdommɑɔ, wi u
bba	wɔllu kɑ ten ɡɑ̃ɑnu tɑkɑ kuɑ,
bba	kɑ tem kɑ mɛn ɡɑ̃ɑnu kɑ mɑɑ
bba	nim wɔ̃ku kɑ ɡen ɡɑ̃ɑnu.
bba	Gɔrɑdo wi, u ɡeruɑ u nɛɛ, sɑɑ
bba	Sɑɑ yɑ turɑ bu kɑ ɡɔribu siri.
bba	Bɑ ye swɑɑ kɑ̃ yu kɑ nɑɑnɛ
bba	dokeobu tɑbu ko kpɑ yu bu tɑbu di.
bba	Bɑ mɑɑ ye yiiko wɛ̃ bweseru
bba	bɑɑteren wɔllɔ, kɑ tɔmbu kpuro
bba	kɑ bɑrum bɑɑmɛre kɑ tem
bba	Bɑ resɛm dɑ̃ɑ bii ni ɡɑmɑ nin
bba	ɡɑmɑ yerɔ wuun biruɔ. Mɑ dɑ̃ɑ
bba	bii ɡɑmɑ yee ten min di yɛm mu
bba	kokɑ mu tɛriɑ sere kilo ɡoobɑ
bba	wunɔbu (300), mɑ mɛn dukum mɑɑ
bba	turɑ sere dumin toro ɡɛndɛɔ.
bba	Yerɑ wɛrɛku ni, nu sinɑmbu kpuro
bba	mɛnnɑ ɡɑm ɡum mi bɑ rɑ soku kɑ
bba	I ye tɔ̃yɑ kɑ nuku sɑnkirɑnu
bba	kɔsio, nɡe mɛ yɑ yen yiiko kɑ
bba	dukiɑn doo nɔɔru di. Domi yɑ yen
bba	tii sɔ̃ɔwɑ yɑ nɛɛ, wee, yɑ
bba	sɔ̃ nɡe sinɑ boko, yɑ ǹ sɑ̃ɑ
bba	ɡɔmini. Mɛyɑ yɑ ǹ mɑɑ nuku
bba	Nɑ mɑɑ wɑ Gusunɔ wɔllɑ wukiɑrɑ
bba	mɑ dum kɑɑ ɡɑɑ kurɑmɑ. Wi u ye
bba	sɔni win yĩsirɑ Gemɡii kɑ
bba	Bɔrɔkini. Gem sɔɔrɑ u rɑ siri,
bba	mɛyɑ u rɑ mɑɑ kɑ tɑbu ko.
bba	U mɑɑ mɑn sɔ̃ɔwɑ u nɛɛ, n yeni
bba	yoruo domi win ɡɑri, ɡɑri ɡeeyɑ,
bba	yi mɑɑ sɑ̃ɑ nɑɑnɛɡii.
bba	Nɛ Yohɑnu nɑ yɑbu yeni nuɑ, nɑ
bba	mɑɑ ye wɑ. Ye nɑ ye nuɑ nɑ ye wɑ
bba	nɑ kpɑ, nɑ kpunɑ wɔllun ɡɔrɑdo
bba	win wuswɑɑɔ wi u mɑn ye kpuro
bba	sɔ̃ɔsi, n kɑ nùn sɑ̃.
